  display: none;
}

  #content-area,

  }

  #table-of-contents li[data-depth="3"] {
    counter-set: h6-counter;
  }

  #content-area h2[id]::before,
  #table-of-contents li[data-depth="0"] a::before {
    counter-increment: h2-counter;
    content: counter(h2-counter) ". ";
  }

  #content-area h3[id]::before,
  #table-of-contents li[data-depth="1"] a::before {
    counter-increment: h3-counter;
    content: counter(h2-counter) "." counter(h3-counter) " ";
  }

  #content-area h4[id]::before,

    counter-increment: h4-counter;

      " ";
  }

  #content-area h5[id]::before,
  #content-area h5::before,

    counter-increment: h5-counter;
    content: counter(h2-counter) "." counter(h3-counter) "." counter(h4-counter)
      "." counter(h5-counter) " ";
  }

your agent or tool.</p></div><div id="page-context-menu" class="flex items-center shrink-0 min-w-[156px] mt-3 sm:hidden"><button id="page-context-menu-button" class="rounded-l-xl px-3 text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300 py-1.5 border border-gray-200 dark:border-white/[0.07] bg-background-light dark:bg-background-dark hover:bg-gray-600/5 dark:hover:bg-gray-200/5 border-r-0" aria-label="Copy page"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-center font-medium"><svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="w-4 h-4"><path stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path><path d="M2.80103 11.998L1.77203 5.07397C1.61003 3.98097 2.36403 2.96397 3.45603 2.80197L10.38 class="group disabled:pointer-events-none [&amp;&gt;span]:line-clamp-1 overflow-hidden group flex items-center py-0.5 gap-1 text-sm text-gray-950/50 dark:text-white/50 group-hover:text-gray-950/70 dark:group-hover:text-white/70 rounded-none rounded-r-xl border px-3 border-gray-200 aspect-square dark:border-white/[0.07] bg-background-light dark:bg-background-dark hover:bg-gray-600/5 dark:hover:bg-gray-200/5" aria-label="More actions" type="button" id="radix-_R_5hmav5tj9rqaabsnpfdb_" aria-haspopup="menu" aria-expanded="false" data-state="closed"><svg width="8" height="24" viewBox="0 -9 3 24" class="transition-transform text-gray-400 overflow-visible group-hover:text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-600 dark:group-hover:text-gray-400 rotate-90"><path d="M0 0L3 3L0 6" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round"></path></svg></button></div></header><div class="mdx-content relative mt-8 mb-14 prose prose-gray dark:prose-invert [contain:inline-size] isolate" data-page-title="Integrate skills into your agent" data-page-href="/integrate-skills" id="content"><span data-as="p">This guide explains how to add skills support to an AI agent or development tool.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="integration-approaches"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#integration-approaches" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Integration approaches</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">The two main approaches to integrating skills are:</span>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Filesystem-based agents</strong> operate within a computer environment (bash/unix) and represent the most capable option. Skills are activated when models issue shell commands like <code>cat /path/to/my-skill/SKILL.md</code>. Bundled resources are accessed through shell commands.</span>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Tool-based agents</strong> function without a dedicated computer environment. Instead, they implement tools allowing models to trigger skills and access bundled assets. The specific tool implementation is up to the developer.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="overview"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#overview" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Overview</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">A skills-compatible agent needs to:</span>
<ol>
<li><strong>Discover</strong> skills in configured directories</li>
<li><strong>Load metadata</strong> (name and description) at startup</li>
<li><strong>Match</strong> user tasks to relevant skills</li>
<li><strong>Activate</strong> skills by loading full instructions</li>
<li><strong>Execute</strong> scripts and access resources as needed</li>
</ol>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="skill-discovery"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#skill-discovery" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Skill discovery</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Skills are folders containing a <code>SKILL.md</code> file. Your agent should scan configured directories for valid skills.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="loading-metadata"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#loading-metadata" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Loading metadata</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">At startup, parse only the frontmatter of each <code>SKILL.md</code> file. This keeps initial context usage low.</span>
<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="parsing-frontmatter"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#parsing-frontmatter" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Parsing frontmatter</span></h3>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group text-gray-950 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border border-gray-950/10 dark:border-white/10 dark:twoslash-dark bg-transparent dark:bg-transparent" numberOfLines="10" language="text"><div data-floating-buttons="true" class="absolute top-3 right-4 flex items-center gap-1.5"><div class="z-10 relative select-none"><button class="h-[26px] w-[26px] flex items-center justify-center rounded-md backdrop-blur peer group/code-snippet-feedback-button" id="code-snippet-feedback-button" aria-label="Report incorrect code"><svg code block"><svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400 group-hover/copy-button:text-gray-500 dark:text-white/40 viewBox="0 0 18 18" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400 group-hover/ask-ai-button:text-gray-500 dark:text-white/40 dark:bg-codeblock relative text-sm leading-6 children:!my-0 children:!shadow-none children:!bg-transparent transition-[height] duration-300 ease-in-out code-block-background [&amp;_*]:ring-0 [&amp;_*]:outline-0 [&amp;_*]:focus:ring-0 [&amp;_*]:focus:outline-0 rounded-2xl bg-white overflow-x-auto scrollbar-thin scrollbar-thumb-rounded scrollbar-thumb-black/15 hover:scrollbar-thumb-black/20 active:scrollbar-thumb-black/20 dark:scrollbar-thumb-white/20 dark:hover:scrollbar-thumb-white/25 dark:active:scrollbar-thumb-white/25" data-component-part="code-block-root" tabindex="0" style="font-variant-ligatures:none;height:auto;background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E"><div class="font-mono whitespace-pre leading-6"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E;color:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4" language="text"><code language="text" numberOfLines="10"><span class="line"><span>function parseMetadata(skillPath):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    content = readFile(skillPath + &quot;/SKILL.md&quot;)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    frontmatter = extractYAMLFrontmatter(content)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    return {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>        name: frontmatter.name,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>        description: frontmatter.description,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>        path: skillPath</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span></code></pre></div></div><div data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="injecting-into-context"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#injecting-into-context" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Injecting into context</span></h3>
<span data-as="p">Include skill metadata in the system prompt so the model knows what skills are available.</span>
<span data-as="p">Follow your platform’s guidance for system prompt updates. For example, for Claude models, the recommended format uses XML:</span>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group text-gray-950 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border border-gray-950/10 dark:border-white/10 dark:twoslash-dark bg-transparent <span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#116329;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">description</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&gt;</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">Extracts text and tables from PDF files, fills forms, merges documents.</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#116329;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">description</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#116329;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">skill</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#116329;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">name</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&gt;</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">data-analysis</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#116329;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">name</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#116329;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">description</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&gt;</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">Analyzes datasets, generates charts, and creates summary reports.</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#116329;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">description</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#116329;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">location</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&gt;</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">/path/to/skills/data-analysis/SKILL.md</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#116329;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">location</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#116329;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">skill</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#116329;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">available_skills</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#808080">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div><div data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p">For filesystem-based agents, include the <code>location</code> field with the absolute path to the SKILL.md file. For tool-based agents, the location can be omitted.</span>
<span data-as="p">Keep metadata concise. Each skill should add roughly 50-100 tokens to the context.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="security-considerations"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#security-considerations" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Security considerations</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Script execution introduces security risks. Consider:</span>
<ul>
<li><strong>Sandboxing</strong>: Run scripts in isolated environments</li>
<li><strong>Allowlisting</strong>: Only execute scripts from trusted skills</li>
<li><strong>Confirmation</strong>: Ask users before running potentially dangerous operations</li>
<li><strong>Logging</strong>: Record all script executions for auditing</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="reference-implementation"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#reference-implementation" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Reference implementation</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">The <a href="https://github.com/agentskills/agentskills/tree/main/skills-ref" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">skills-ref</a> library provides Python utilities and a CLI for working with skills.</span>
<span data-as="p">For example:</span>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Validate a skill directory:</strong></span>

validate &lt;path&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span></code></pre></div></div><div data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Generate <code>&lt;available_skills&gt;</code> XML for agent prompts:</strong></span>
